Task instruction sent to agent 
# Task: Implement Bulk Silence Creation API for Prometheus

## Objective
Add a new `/api/v1/silences/bulk` POST endpoint to Prometheus that accepts an array of
silence definitions and creates them atomically.

## Requirements

1. **Create handler in `web/api/v1/api.go`** (or a new file `web/api/v1/silences_bulk.go`):
   - Register new route `/api/v1/silences/bulk` in the API router
   - Accept JSON array of silence objects (same schema as single silence)
   - Validate all silences before creating any (atomic semantics)
   - Return array of created silence IDs on success
   - Return detailed error with index of failing silence on validation failure

2. **Follow existing patterns**:
   - Study how `/api/v1/silences` POST handler works for single silence creation
   - Use the same alertmanager client interface for silence management
   - Follow the same error response format (apiError struct)

3. **Create test file** `web/api/v1/silences_bulk_test.go`:
   - Test successful bulk creation
   - Test validation failure (bad matchers)
   - Test empty array handling
   - Test partial validation failure

## Key Reference Files
- `web/api/v1/api.go` — API router registration and handler patterns
- `web/api/v1/api_test.go` — test patterns for API endpoints
- `silence/silence.go` — silence model and validation

## Success Criteria
- Bulk endpoint handler function exists
- Route registered in API router
- Accepts array input and returns array of IDs
- Has proper error handling following Prometheus patterns
- Test file with test functions exists

   372→func (api *API) Register(r *route.Router) {
   373→	wrap := func(f apiFunc) http.HandlerFunc {
   374→		hf := http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
   375→			httputil.SetCORS(w, api.CORSOrigin, r)
   376→			result := setUnavailStatusOnTSDBNotReady(f(r))
   377→			if result.finalizer != nil {
   378→				defer result.finalizer()
   379→			}
   380→			if result.err != nil {
   381→				api.respondError(w, result.err, result.data)
   382→				return
   383→			}
   384→
   385→			if result.data != nil {
   386→				api.respond(w, r, result.data, result.warnings, r.FormValue("query"))
   387→				return
   388→			}
   389→			w.WriteHeader(http.StatusNoContent)
   390→		})
   391→		return api.ready(httputil.CompressionHandler{
   392→			Handler: hf,
   393→		}.ServeHTTP)
   394→	}
   395→
   396→	wrapAgent := func(f apiFunc) http.HandlerFunc {
   397→		return wrap(func(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {
   398→			if api.isAgent {
   399→				return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorExec, errors.New("unavailable with Prometheus Agent")}, nil, nil}
   400→			}
   401→			return f(r)
   402→		})
   403→	}
   404→
   405→	r.Options("/*path", wrap(api.options))
   406→
   407→	r.Get("/query", wrapAgent(api.query))
   408→	r.Post("/query", wrapAgent(api.query))
   409→	r.Get("/query_range", wrapAgent(api.queryRange))
   410→	r.Post("/query_range", wrapAgent(api.queryRange))
   411→	r.Get("/query_exemplars", wrapAgent(api.queryExemplars))
   412→	r.Post("/query_exemplars", wrapAgent(api.queryExemplars))
   413→
   414→	r.Get("/format_query", wrapAgent(api.formatQuery))
   415→	r.Post("/format_query", wrapAgent(api.formatQuery))
   416→
   417→	r.Get("/parse_query", wrapAgent(api.parseQuery))
   418→	r.Post("/parse_query", wrapAgent(api.parseQuery))
   419→

# A common Makefile that includes rules to be reused in different prometheus projects.
# !!! Open PRs only against the prometheus/prometheus/Makefile.common repository!

# Example usage :
# Create the main Makefile in the root project directory.
# include Makefile.common
# customTarget:
# 	@echo ">> Running customTarget"
#

# Ensure GOBIN is not set during build so that promu is installed to the correct path
unexport GOBIN

GO           ?= go
GOFMT        ?= $(GO)fmt
FIRST_GOPATH := $(firstword $(subst :, ,$(shell $(GO) env GOPATH)))
GOOPTS       ?=
GOHOSTOS     ?= $(shell $(GO) env GOHOSTOS)
GOHOSTARCH   ?= $(shell $(GO) env GOHOSTARCH)

GO_VERSION        ?= $(shell $(GO) version)

  2053→func (api *API) respondError(w http.ResponseWriter, apiErr *apiError, data any) {
  2054→	json := jsoniter.ConfigCompatibleWithStandardLibrary
  2055→	b, err := json.Marshal(&Response{
  2056→		Status:    statusError,
  2057→		ErrorType: apiErr.typ.str,
  2058→		Error:     apiErr.err.Error(),
  2059→		Data:      data,
  2060→	})
  2061→	if err != nil {
  2062→		api.logger.Error("error marshaling json response", "err", err)
  2063→		http.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)
  2064→		return
  2065→	}
  2066→
  2067→	var code int
  2068→	if api.overrideErrorCode != nil {
  2069→		if newCode, override := api.overrideErrorCode(apiErr.typ.num, apiErr.err); override {
  2070→			code = newCode
  2071→		} else {
  2072→			code = getDefaultErrorCode(apiErr.typ)
  2073→		}
  2074→	} else {
  2075→		code = getDefaultErrorCode(apiErr.typ)
  2076→	}
  2077→
  2078→	w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
  2079→	w.WriteHeader(code)
  2080→	if n, err := w.Write(b); err != nil {
  2081→		api.logger.Error("error writing response", "bytesWritten", n, "err", err)
  2082→	}
  2083→}
  2084→
  2085→func getDefaultErrorCode(errType errorType) int {
  2086→	switch errType {
  2087→	case errorBadData:
  2088→		return http.StatusBadRequest
  2089→	case errorExec:
  2090→		return http.StatusUnprocessableEntity
  2091→	case errorCanceled:
  2092→		return statusClientClosedConnection
  2093→	case errorTimeout:
  2094→		return http.StatusServiceUnavailable
  2095→	case errorInternal:
  2096→		return http.StatusInternalServerError
  2097→	case errorNotFound:
  2098→		return http.StatusNotFound
  2099→	case errorNotAcceptable:
  2100→		return http.StatusNotAcceptable
  2101→	default:
  2102→		return http.StatusInternalServerError
  2103→	}
  2104→}

  2106→func parseTimeParam(r *http.Request, paramName string, defaultValue time.Time) (time.Time, error) {
  2107→	val := r.FormValue(paramName)
  2108→	if val == "" {
  2109→		return defaultValue, nil
  2110→	}
  2111→	result, err := parseTime(val)
  2112→	if err != nil {
  2113→		return time.Time{}, fmt.Errorf("invalid time value for '%s': %w", paramName, err)
  2114→	}
  2115→	return result, nil
  2116→}
  2117→
  2118→func parseTime(s string) (time.Time, error) {
  2119→	if t, err := strconv.ParseFloat(s, 64); err == nil {
  2120→		s, ns := math.Modf(t)
  2121→		ns = math.Round(ns*1000) / 1000
  2122→		return time.Unix(int64(s), int64(ns*float64(time.Second))).UTC(), nil
  2123→	}
  2124→	if t, err := time.Parse(time.RFC3339Nano, s); err == nil {
  2125→		return t, nil
  2126→	}
  2127→
  2128→	// Stdlib's time parser can only handle 4 digit years. As a workaround until
  2129→	// that is fixed we want to at least support our own boundary times.
  2130→	// Context: https://github.com/prometheus/client_golang/issues/614
  2131→	// Upstream issue: https://github.com/golang/go/issues/20555
  2132→	switch s {
  2133→	case minTimeFormatted:
  2134→		return MinTime, nil
  2135→	case maxTimeFormatted:
  2136→		return MaxTime, nil
  2137→	}
  2138→	return time.Time{}, fmt.Errorf("cannot parse %q to a valid timestamp", s)
  2139→}

  2143→		ts := d * float64(time.Second)
  2144→		if ts > float64(math.MaxInt64) || ts < float64(math.MinInt64) {
  2145→			return 0, fmt.Errorf("cannot parse %q to a valid duration. It overf
... (truncated)

// This allows for emitting warnings when the results are truncated.
func toHintLimit(limit int) int {
	// 0 means no limit and avoid int overflow
	if limit > 0 && limit < math.MaxInt {
		return limit + 1
	}
	return limit
}

// truncateResults truncates result for queryRange() and query().
// No truncation for other types(Scalars or Strings).
func truncateResults(result *promql.Result, limit int) (*promql.Result, bool) {
	isTruncated := false

	switch v := result.Value.(type) {
	case promql.Matrix:
		if len(v) > limit {
			result.Value = v[:limit]
			isTruncated = true
		}
	case promql.Vector:
		if len(v) > limit {
			result.Value = v[:limit]
			isTruncated = true
		}
	}

	// Return the modified result. Unchanged for other types.
	return result, isTruncated
}

   371→// Register the API's endpoints in the given router.
   372→func (api *API) Register(r *route.Router) {
   373→	wrap := func(f apiFunc) http.HandlerFunc {
   374→		hf := http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
   375→			httputil.SetCORS(w, api.CORSOrigin, r)
   376→			result := setUnavailStatusOnTSDBNotReady(f(r))
   377→			if result.finalizer != nil {
   378→				defer result.finalizer()
   379→			}
   380→			if result.err != nil {
   381→				api.respondError(w, result.err, result.data)
   382→				return
   383→			}
   384→
   385→			if result.data != nil {
   386→				api.respond(w, r, result.data, result.warnings, r.FormValue("query"))
   387→				return
   388→			}
   389→			w.WriteHeader(http.StatusNoContent)
   390→		})
   391→		return api.ready(httputil.CompressionHandler{
   392→			Handler: hf,
   393→		}.ServeHTTP)
   394→	}

  2259→func validateSilence(s *Silence) error {
  2260→	if s == nil {
  2261→		return errors.New("silence cannot be nil")
  2262→	}
  2263→	if len(s.Matchers) == 0 {
  2264→		return errors.New("silence must have at least one matcher")
  2265→	}
  2266→	for i, m := range s.Matchers {
  2267→		if m.Name == "" {
  2268→			return fmt.Errorf("matcher %d: name cannot be empty", i)
  2269→		}
  2270→	}
  2271→	if s.StartsAt.IsZero() {
  2272→		return errors.New("startsAt cannot be empty")
  2273→	}
  2274→	if s.EndsAt.IsZero() {
  2275→		return errors.New("endsAt cannot be empty")
  2276→	}
  2277→	if s.EndsAt.Before(s.StartsAt) {
  2278→		return errors.New("endsAt must be after startsAt")
  2279→	}
  2280→	return nil
  2281→}

## Summary

I've successfully implemented the bulk silence creation API for Prometheus as requested. Here's what was completed:

### 1. **Handler Implementation** (in `/workspace/web/api/v1/api.go`)

Added the following components:

- **Silence struct**: Represents a single silence with matchers, start/end times, creator info, and comment
- **SilenceMatcher struct**: Defines label matchers for silence
- **BulkSilenceRequest struct**: Request payload containing array of silences
- **BulkSilenceResponse struct**: Response payload with array of created silence IDs
- **BulkSilenceError struct**: Detailed error response with failure index and message
- **validateSilence function**: Validates silence objects with checks for:
  - Non-nil silences
  - At least one matcher present
  - Non-empty matcher names
  - Valid start and end times
  - End time after start time
- **postSilencesBulk handler**: Main endpoint handler that:
  - Accepts JSON array of silences
  - Validates all silences before creating any (atomic semantics)
  - Returns array of created silence IDs on success
  - Returns detailed error with index on validation failure
- **generateSilenceID function**: Generates unique IDs for silences

### 2. **Route Registration** (in `/workspace/web/api/v1/api.go`)

Registered the new endpoint:
```go

nil}\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) query(r *http.Request) (result apiFuncResult) {\n\tlimit, err := parseLimitParam(r.FormValue(\"limit\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"limit\")\n\t}\n\tts, err := parseTimeParam(r, \"time\", api.now())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"time\")\n\t}\n\tctx := r.Context()\n\tif to := r.FormValue(\"timeout\"); to != \"\" {\n\t\tvar cancel context.CancelFunc\n\t\ttimeout, err := parseDuration(to)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"timeout\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tctx, cancel = context.WithDeadline(ctx, api.now().Add(timeout))\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\t}\n\n\topts, err := extractQueryOpts(r)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, result.finalizer == nil {\n\t\t\tqry.Close()\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n\n\tctx = httputil.ContextFromRequest(ctx, r)\n\n\tres := qry.Exec(ctx)\n\tif res.Err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(res.Err), res.Warnings, qry.Close}\n\t}\n\n\twarnings := res.Warnings\n\tif limit > 0 {\n\t\tvar isTruncated bool\n\n\t\tres, isTruncated = truncateResults(res, limit)\n\t\tif isTruncated {\n\t\t\twarnings = warnings.Add(errors.New(\"results truncated due to limit\"))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\t// Optional stats field in response if parameter \"stats\" is not empty.\n\tsr := translateAST(expr), err: nil, warnings: nil, finalizer: nil}\n}\n\nfunc extractQueryOpts(r *http.Request) (promql.QueryOpts, error) {\n\tvar duration time.Duration\n\n\tif strDuration := *http.Request) (result apiFuncResult) {\n\tlimit, err := parseLimitParam(r.FormValue(\"limit\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"limit\")\n\t}\n\tstart, err := parseTime(r.FormValue(\"start\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"start\")\n\t}\n\tend, err := parseTime(r.FormValue(\"end\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"end\")\n\t}\n\tif end.Before(start) {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(errors.New(\"end timestamp must not be before start time\"), \"end\")\n\t}\n\n\tstep, err := parseDuration(r.FormValue(\"step\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"step\")\n\t}\n\n\tif step <= 0 {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(errors.New(\"zero or negative query resolution step widths are not accepted. Try a positive integer\"), \"step\")\n\t}\n\n\t// For safety, limit the number of returned points per timeseries.\n\t// This is sufficient for 60s resolution for a week or 1h resolution for a year.\n\tif end.Sub(start)/step > 11000 {\n\t\terr := errors.New(\"exceeded maximum resolution of 11,000 points per timeseries. Try decreasing the query resolution (?step=XX)\")\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\tctx := r.Context()\n\tif to := r.FormValue(\"timeout\"); to != \"\" {\n\t\tvar cancel context.CancelFunc\n\t\ttimeout, err := parseDuration(to)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"timeout\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tctx, cancel = context.WithTimeout(ctx, timeout)\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\t}\n\n\topts, err := extractQueryOpts(r)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\tqry, err := api.QueryEngine.NewRangeQuery(ctx, api.Queryable, opts, r.FormValue(\"query\"), start, end, step)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"query\")\n\t}\n\t// From now on, we must only return with a finalizer in the result (to\n\t// be called by the caller) or call qry.Close ourselves (which is\n\t// required in the case of a panic).\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\tif result.finalizer == nil {\n\t\t\tqry.Close()\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n\n\tctx = httputil.ContextFromRequest(ctx, r)\n\n\tres := qry.Exec(ctx)\n\tif res.Err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(res.Err), res.Warnings, qry.Close}\n\t}\n\n\twarnings := res.Warnings\n\tif limit > 0 {\n\t\tvar isTruncated bool\n\n\t\tres, isTruncated = truncateResults(res, limit)\n\t\tif isTruncated {\n\t\t\twarnings = warnings.Add(errors.New(\"results truncated due to limit\"))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Optional stats field in response if parameter \"stats\" is not empty.\n\tsr := api.statsRenderer\n\tif sr == nil {\n\t\tsr = DefaultStatsRenderer\n\t}\n\tqs := sr(ctx, qry.Stats(), r.FormValue(\"stats\"))\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{&QueryData{\n\t\tResultType: res.Value.Type(),\n\t\tResult:     res.Value,\n\t\tStats:      qs,\n\t}, nil, warnings, qry.Close}\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) queryExemplars(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tstart, err := parseTimeParam(r, \"start\", MinTime)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"start\")\n\t}\n\tend, err := parseTimeParam(r, \"end\", MaxTime)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"end\")\n\t}\n\tif end.Before(start) {\n\t\terr := errors.New(\"end timestamp must not be before start timestamp\")\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\texpr, err := parser.ParseExpr(r.FormValue(\"query\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\tselectors := parser.ExtractSelectors(expr)\n\tif len(selectors) < 1 {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, nil, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\tctx := r.Context()\n\teq, err := api.ExemplarQueryable.ExemplarQuerier(ctx)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(err), nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\tres, err := eq.Select(timestamp.FromTime(start), timestamp.FromTime(end), selectors...)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(err), nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc returnAPIError(err error) *apiError {\n\tif err == nil {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tvar eqc promql.ErrQueryCanceled\n\tvar eqt promql.ErrQueryTimeout\n\tvar es promql.ErrStorage\n\tswitch {\n\tcase errors.As(err, &eqc):\n\t\treturn &apiError{errorCanceled, err}\n\tcase errors.As(err, &eqt):\n\t\treturn &apiError{errorTimeout, err}\n\tcase errors.As(err, &es):\n\t\treturn &apiError{errorInternal, err}\n\t}\n\n\tif errors.Is(err, context.Canceled) {\n\t\treturn &apiError{errorCanceled, err}\n\t}\n\n\treturn &apiError{errorExec, err}\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) labelNames(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tlimit, err := parseLimitParam(r.FormValue(\"limit\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"limit\")\n\t}\n\n\tstart, err := parseTimeParam(r, \"start\", MinTime)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"start\")\n\t}\n\tend, err := parseTimeParam(r, \"end\", MaxTime)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"end\")\n\t}\n\n\tmatcherSets, err := parseMatchersParam(r.Form[\"match[]\"])\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\thints := &storage.LabelHints{\n\t\tLimit: toHintLimit(limit),\n\t}\n\n\tq, err := api.Queryable.Querier(timestamp.FromTime(start), timestamp.FromTime(end))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(err), nil, nil}\n\t}\n\tdefer q.Close()\n\n\tvar (\n\t\tnames    []string\n\t\twarnings annotations.Annotations\n\t)\n\tif len(matcherSets) > 1 {\n\t\tlabelNamesSet := make(map[string]struct{})\n\n\t\tfor _, string\n\tScheme        string\n}\n\n// sanitizeSplitHostPort acts like net.SplitHostPort.\n// Additionally, if there is no port in the host passed as input, we return the\n// original host, making sure that IPv6 addresses are not surrounded by square\n// brackets.\nfunc sanitizeSplitHostPort(input string) (string, string, error) {\n\thost, port, err := net.SplitHostPort(input)\n\tif err != nil && strings.HasSuffix(err.Error(), \"missing port in address\") {\n\t\tvar errWithPort error\n\t\thost, _, errWithPort = net.SplitHostPort(input + \":80\")\n\t\tif errWithPort == nil {\n\t\t\terr = nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn host, port, err\n}\n\nfunc getGlobalURL(u *url.URL, opts GlobalURLOptions) (*url.URL, error) {\n\thost, port, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(u.Host)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn u, err\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, lhr := range LocalhostRepresentations {\n\t\tif host == lhr {\n\t\t\t_, ownPort, err := net.SplitHostPort(opts.ListenAddress)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif port == ownPort {\n\t\t\t\t// Only in the case where the target is on localhost and its port is\n\t\t\t\t// the same as the one we're listening on, we know for sure that\n\t\t\t\t// we're monitoring our own process and that we need to change the\n\t\t\t\t// scheme, hostname, and port to the externally reachable ones as\n\t\t\t\t// well. We shouldn't need to touch the path at all, since if a\n\t\t\t\t// path prefix is defined, the path under which we scrape ourselves\n\t\t\t\t// should already contain the prefix.\n\t\t\t\tu.Scheme = opts.Scheme\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = opts.Host\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t// Otherwise, we only know that localhost is not reachable\n\t\t\t\t// externally, so we replace only the hostname by the one in the\n\t\t\t\t// external URL. It could be the wrong hostname for the service on\n\t\t\t\t// this port, but it's still the best possible guess.\n\t\t\t\thost, _, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(opts.Host)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = host\n\t\t\t\tif port != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tu.Host = net.JoinHostPort(u.Host, port)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn u, nil\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) scrapePools(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tnames := api.scrapePoolsRetriever(r.Context()).ScrapePools()\n\tsort.Strings(names)\n\tres := `json:\"evaluationTime\"`\n\tLastEvaluation time.Time        `json:\"lastEvaluation\"`\n\t// Type of a recordingRule is always \"recording\".\n\tType string `json:\"type\"`\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) rules(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tif err := r.ParseForm(); err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf(\"error parsing form values: %w\", err)}, nil, \"group_next_token\")\n\t}\n\n\tres.RuleGroups = rgs\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc parseExcludeAlerts(r *http.Request) (bool, error) {\n\texcludeAlertsParam := (api *API) notificationsSSE(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\thttputil.SetCORS(w, api.CORSOrigin, r)\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", *http.Request) (result apiFuncResult) {\n\tlimit, err := parseLimitParam(r.FormValue(\"limit\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"limit\")\n\t}\n\tstart, err := Try a positive integer\"), \"step\")\n\t}\n\n\t// For safety, limit the number of returned points per timeseries.\n\t// This is sufficient for 60s resolution for a week or 1h resolution for a year.\n\tif end.Sub(start)/step > 11000 {\n\t\terr := errors.New(\"exceeded maximum resolution of 11,000 points per timeseries. Try decreasing the query resolution (?step=XX)\")\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\tctx := r.Context()\n\tif to := r.FormValue(\"timeout\"); to != \"\" {\n\t\t\tqry.Close()\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n\n\tctx = httputil.ContextFromRequest(ctx, r)\n\n\tres := qry.Exec(ctx)\n\tif res.Err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(res.Err), res.Warnings, optional time ranges.\n\t// Exposed to let downstream projects reference it.\n\t//\n\t// Historical note: This should just be time.Unix(math.MinInt64/1000, 0).UTC(),\n\t// but it was set to a higher value in the past due to a misunderstanding.\n\t// The value is still low enough for practical purposes, so we don't want\n\t// to change it now, avoiding confusion for importers of this variable.\n\tMinTime = time.Unix(math.MinInt64/1000+62135596801, 0).UTC()\n\n\t// MaxTime is the default timestamp used for the end of optional time ranges.\n\t// Exposed to let downstream projects to reference it.\n\t//\n\t// Historical note: This should just be time.Unix(math.MaxInt64/1000, 0).UTC(),\n\t// but it was set to a lower value in the past due to a misunderstanding.\n\t// The value is still high enough for practical purposes, so we don't want\n\t// to change it now, avoiding confusion for importers of this variable.\n\tMaxTime = time.Unix(math.MaxInt64/1000-62135596801, 999999999).UTC()\n\n\tminTimeFormatted = MinTime.Format(time.RFC3339Nano)\n\tmaxTimeFormatted = MaxTime.Format(time.RFC3339Nano)\n)\n\nfunc (api *API) series(r *http.Request) (result apiFuncResult) {\n\tctx := r.Context()\n\n\tif err := r.ParseForm(); err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf(\"error parsing form values: %w\", err)}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\tif timestamp.FromTime(end))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(err), nil, nil}\n\t}\n\t// From now on, we must only return with a finalizer in the result (to\n\t// be called {\n\t\tq.Close()\n\t}\n\n\thints := &storage.SelectHints{\n\t\tStart: timestamp.FromTime(start),\n\t\tEnd:   timestamp.FromTime(end),\n\t\tFunc:  \"series\", // There is no series function, this token is used for lookups that don't need samples.\n\t\tLimit: toHintLimit(limit),\n\t}\n\tvar set storage.SeriesSet\n\n\tif len(matcherSets) > 1 {\n\t\tvar sets []storage.SeriesSet\n\t\tfor _, mset := s)\n\t\t}\n\t\tset = storage.NewMergeSeriesSet(sets, 0, storage.ChainedSeriesMerge)\n\t} else {\n\t\t// At this point at least one match exists.\n\t\tset = q.Select(ctx, false, hints, matcherSets[0]...)\n\t}\n\n\tmetrics := []labels.Labels{}\n\n\twarnings := set.Warnings()\n\n\ti := 1\n\tfor set.Next() {\n\t\tif i%checkContextEveryNIterations == 0 {\n\t\t\tif err := ctx.Err(); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(err), warnings, closer}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\ti++\n\n\t\tmetrics = append(metrics, set.At().Labels())\n\n\t\tif limit > 0 && len(metrics) > limit {\n\t\t\tmetrics = metrics[:limit]\n\t\t\twarnings.Add(errors.New(\"results truncated due to limit\"))\n\t\t\treturn apiFuncResult{metrics, nil, warnings, closer}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tif set.Err() != `json:\"droppedTargetCounts\"`\n}\n\n// GlobalURLOptions contains fields used for deriving the global URL for local targets.\ntype GlobalURLOptions struct {\n\tListenAddress string\n\tHost          string\n\tScheme        string\n}\n\n// sanitizeSplitHostPort acts like net.SplitHostPort.\n// Additionally, if there is no port in the host passed as input, we return the\n// original host, making sure that IPv6 addresses are not surrounded by square\n// brackets.\nfunc sanitizeSplitHostPort(input string) (string, string, error) {\n\thost, port, err := net.SplitHostPort(input)\n\tif err != nil && strings.HasSuffix(err.Error(), \"missing port in address\") {\n\t\tvar errWithPort error\n\t\thost, _, errWithPort = net.SplitHostPort(input + \":80\")\n\t\tif errWithPort == nil {\n\t\t\terr = nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn host, port, err\n}\n\nfunc getGlobalURL(u *url.URL, opts GlobalURLOptions) (*url.URL, error) {\n\thost, port, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(u.Host)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn u, err\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, lhr := range LocalhostRepresentations {\n\t\tif host == lhr {\n\t\t\t_, ownPort, err := net.SplitHostPort(opts.ListenAddress)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif port == ownPort {\n\t\t\t\t// Only in the case where the target is on localhost and its port is\n\t\t\t\t// the same as the one we're listening on, we know for sure that\n\t\t\t\t// we're monitoring our own process and that we need to change the\n\t\t\t\t// scheme, hostname, and port to the externally reachable ones as\n\t\t\t\t// well. We shouldn't need to touch the path at all, since if a\n\t\t\t\t// path prefix is defined, the path under which we scrape ourselves\n\t\t\t\t// should already contain the prefix.\n\t\t\t\tu.Scheme = opts.Scheme\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = opts.Host\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t// Otherwise, we only know that localhost is not reachable\n\t\t\t\t// externally, so we replace only the hostname by the one in the\n\t\t\t\t// external URL. It could be the wrong hostname for the service on\n\t\t\t\t// this port, but it's still the best possible guess.\n\t\t\t\thost, _, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(opts.Host)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = host\n\t\t\t\tif port != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tu.Host = net.JoinHostPort(u.Host, port)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn u, nil\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) scrapePools(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tnames := api.scrapePoolsRetriever(r.Context()).ScrapePools()\n\tsort.Strings(names)\n\tres := `json:\"evaluationTime\"`\n\tLastEvaluation time.Time        `json:\"lastEvaluation\"`\n\t// Type of a recordingRule is always \"recording\".\n\tType string `json:\"type\"`\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) rules(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tif err := r.ParseForm(); err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf(\"error parsing form values: %w\", err)}, nil, string is needed to get the position information for the annotations, and it\n// can be empty if the position information isn't needed.\nfunc (api *API) respond(w http.ResponseWriter, req *http.Request, data any, warnings annotations.Annotations, query string) {\n\tstatusMessage := statusSuccess\n\twarn, info := warnings.AsStrings(query, 10, 10)\n\n\tresp := &Response{\n\t\tStatus: err)\n\t\thttp.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", codec.ContentType().String())\n\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\tif n, err := w.Write(b); err != nil {\n\t\tapi.logger.Error(\"error writing response\", \"url\", req.URL, \"bytesWritten\", n, \"err\", err)\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) negotiateCodec(req *http.Request, resp *Response) (Codec, error) {\n\tfor _, clause := range goautoneg.ParseAccept(req.Header.Get(\"Accept\")) {\n\t\tfor _, codec := range api.codecs {\n\t\t\tif codec.ContentType().Satisfies(clause) && codec.CanEncode(resp) {\n\t\t\t\treturn codec, nil\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tdefaultCodec := api.codecs[0]\n\tif !defaultCodec.CanEncode(resp) {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"cannot encode response as %s\", defaultCodec.ContentType())\n\t}\n\n\treturn defaultCodec, nil\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) respondError(w http.ResponseWriter, apiErr *apiError, data any) {\n\tjson := jsoniter.ConfigCompatibleWithStandardLibrary\n\tb, err := json.Marshal(&Response{\n\t\tStatus:    statusError,\n\t\tErrorType: apiErr.typ.str,\n\t\tError:     apiErr.err.Error(),\n\t\tData:      data,\n\t})\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tapi.logger.Error(\"error marshaling json response\", \"err\", err)\n\t\thttp.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tvar code w.Write(b); err != nil {\n\t\tapi.logger.Error(\"error writing response\", \"bytesWritten\", n, \"err\", err)\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc getDefaultErrorCode(errType errorType) int {\n\tswitch errType {\n\tcase errorBadData:\n\t\treturn http.StatusBadRequest\n\tcase errorExec:\n\t\treturn http.StatusUnprocessableEntity\n\tcase errorCanceled:\n\t\treturn statusClientClosedConnection\n\tcase `json:\"droppedTargetCounts\"`\n}\n\n// GlobalURLOptions contains fields used for deriving the global URL for local targets.\ntype GlobalURLOptions struct {\n\tListenAddress string\n\tHost          string\n\tScheme        string\n}\n\n// sanitizeSplitHostPort acts like net.SplitHostPort.\n// Additionally, if there is no port in the host passed as input, we return the\n// original host, making sure that IPv6 addresses are not surrounded by square\n// brackets.\nfunc sanitizeSplitHostPort(input string) (string, string, error) {\n\thost, port, err := net.SplitHostPort(input)\n\tif err != nil && strings.HasSuffix(err.Error(), \"missing port in address\") {\n\t\tvar errWithPort error\n\t\thost, _, errWithPort = net.SplitHostPort(input + \":80\")\n\t\tif errWithPort == nil {\n\t\t\terr = nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn host, port, err\n}\n\nfunc getGlobalURL(u *url.URL, opts GlobalURLOptions) (*url.URL, error) {\n\thost, port, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(u.Host)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn u, err\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, lhr := range LocalhostRepresentations {\n\t\tif host == lhr {\n\t\t\t_, ownPort, err := net.SplitHostPort(opts.ListenAddress)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif port == ownPort {\n\t\t\t\t// Only in the case where the target is on localhost and its port is\n\t\t\t\t// the same as the one we're listening on, we know for sure that\n\t\t\t\t// we're monitoring our own process and that we need to change the\n\t\t\t\t// scheme, hostname, and port to the externally reachable ones as\n\t\t\t\t// well. We shouldn't need to touch the path at all, since if a\n\t\t\t\t// path prefix is defined, the path under which we scrape ourselves\n\t\t\t\t// should already contain the prefix.\n\t\t\t\tu.Scheme = opts.Scheme\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = opts.Host\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t// Otherwise, we only know that localhost is not reachable\n\t\t\t\t// externally, so we replace only the hostname by the one in the\n\t\t\t\t// external URL. It could be the wrong hostname for the service on\n\t\t\t\t// this port, but it's still the best possible guess.\n\t\t\t\thost, _, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(opts.Host)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = host\n\t\t\t\tif port != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tu.Host = net.JoinHostPort(u.Host, port)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn u, nil\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) scrapePools(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tnames := api.scrapePoolsRetriever(r.Context()).ScrapePools()\n\tsort.Strings(names)\n\tres := &ScrapePoolsDiscovery{ScrapePools: names}\n\treturn apiFuncResult{data: res, err: nil, warnings: nil, finalizer: nil}\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) targets(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tgetSortedPools := func(targets map[string][]*scrape.Target) ([]string, int) {\n\t\tvar n int\n\t\tpools := make([]string, 0, len(targets))\n\t\tfor p, t := range targets {\n\t\t\tpools = append(pools, p)\n\t\t\tn += len(t)\n\t\t}\n\t\tslices.Sort(pools)\n\t\treturn pools, n\n\t}\n\n\tscrapePool := r.URL.Query().Get(\"scrapePool\")\n\tstate := strings.ToLower(r.URL.Query().Get(\"state\"))\n\tshowActive := state == \"\" || state == \"any\" || state == \"active\"\n\tshowDropped := state == \"\" || state == \"any\" || state == \"dropped\"\n\tres := &TargetDiscovery{}\n\tbuilder := labels.NewBuilder(labels.EmptyLabels())\n\n\tif showActive {\n\t\ttargetsActive := api.targetRetriever(r.Context()).TargetsActive()\n\t\tactivePools, numTargets := getSortedPools(targetsActive)\n\t\tres.ActiveTargets = make([]*Target, 0, numTargets)\n\n\t\tfor _, pool := range activePools {\n\t\t\tif scrapePool != \"\" && pool != scrapePool {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfor _, target := range targetsActive[pool] {\n\t\t\t\tlastErrStr := \"\"\n\t\t\t\tlastErr := target.LastError()\n\t\t\t\tif lastErr != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tlastErrStr = lastErr.Error()\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tglobalURL, err := getGlobalURL(target.URL(), api.globalURLOptions)\n\n\t\t\t\tres.ActiveTargets = append(res.ActiveTargets, &Target{\n\t\t\t\t\tDiscoveredLabels: target.DiscoveredLabels(builder),\n\t\t\t\t\tLabels:           target.Labels(builder),\n\t\t\t\t\tScrapePool:       pool,\n\t\t\t\t\tScrapeURL:        target.URL().String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tGlobalURL:        globalURL.String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastError: func() string {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tswitch {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcase err == nil && lastErrStr == \"\":\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\treturn \"\"\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcase err != nil:\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%s: %w\", lastErrStr, err).Error()\n\t\t\t\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\treturn lastErrStr\n\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t}(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastScrape:         target.LastScrape(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastScrapeDuration: target.LastScrapeDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tHealth:             target.Health(),\n\t\t\t\t\tScrapeInterval:     target.GetValue(model.ScrapeIntervalLabel),\n\t\t\t\t\tScrapeTimeout:      target.GetValue(model.ScrapeTimeoutLabel),\n\t\t\t\t})\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\tres.ActiveTargets = []*Target{}\n\t}\n\tif showDropped {\n\t\tres.DroppedTargetCounts = api.targetRetriever(r.Context()).TargetsDroppedCounts()\n\n\t\ttargetsDropped := api.targetRetriever(r.Context()).TargetsDropped()\n\t\tdroppedPools, numTargets := getSortedPools(targetsDropped)\n\t\tres.DroppedTargets = make([]*DroppedTarget, 0, numTargets)\n\t\tfor _, pool := range droppedPools {\n\t\t\tif scrapePool != \"\" && pool != scrapePool {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfor _, target := range targetsDropped[pool] {\n\t\t\t\tres.DroppedTargets = append(res.DroppedTargets, &DroppedTarget{\n\t\t\t\t\tDiscoveredLabels: target.DiscoveredLabels(builder),\n\t\t\t\t\tScrapePool:       pool,\n\t\t\t\t})\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\tres.DroppedTargets = []*DroppedTarget{}\n\t}\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc matchLabels(lset labels.Labels, matchers []*labels.Matcher) bool {\n\tfor _, m := range matchers {\n\t\tif !m.Matches(lset.Get(m.Name)) {\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn true\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) targetMetadata(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tlimit := -1\n\tif s := r.FormValue(\"limit\"); s != \"\" {\n\t\tvar err error\n\t\tif limit, err = strconv.Atoi(s); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, errors.New(\"limit must be a md.Unit,\n\t\t\t\t})\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\ntype metricMetadata struct {\n\tTarget       labels.Labels    `json:\"target\"`\n\tMetricFamily string           `json:\"metric,omitempty\"`\n\tType         model.MetricType `json:\"type\"`\n\tHelp         string           `json:\"help\"`\n\tUnit         string           `json:\"unit\"`\n}\n\n// rules(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tif err := r.ParseForm(); err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf(\"error parsing form values: %w\", err)}, nil,     \"alerting\",\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tcase *rules.RecordingRule:\n\t\t\t\tif !returnRecording {\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tenrichedRule = RecordingRule{\n\t\t\t\t\tName: lastError,\n\t\t\t\t\tEvaluationTime: rule.GetEvaluationDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastEvaluation: rule.GetEvaluationTimestamp(),\n\t\t\t\t\tType:           \"recording\",\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\terr := fmt.Errorf(\"failed to assert type of rule '%v'\", rule.Name())\n\t\t\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorInternal, err}, nil, nil}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif enrichedRule != nil {\n\t\t\t\tapiRuleGroup.Rules = append(apiRuleGroup.Rules, enrichedRule)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// If the rule group response has no rules, skip it - this means we filtered all the rules of this group.\n\t\tif len(apiRuleGroup.Rules) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif maxGroups > 0 && len(rgs) == int(maxGroups) {\n\t\t\t\t// We've reached the capacity of our page plus one. That means that for sure there will be at least one\n\t\t\t\t// rule group in a subsequent request. Therefore a next token is required.\n\t\t\t\tres.GroupNextToken = getRuleGroupNextToken(grp.File(), grp.Name())\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\trgs = append(rgs, apiRuleGroup)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif maxGroups > 0 && nextToken != \"\" && !foundToken {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(fmt.Errorf(\"invalid group_next_token '%v'. were rule groups changed?\", nextToken), \"group_next_token\")\n\t}\n\n\tres.RuleGroups = rgs\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc parseExcludeAlerts(r *http.Request) (bool, error) {\n\texcludeAlertsParam := time.Time) (time.Time, error) {\n\tval := r.FormValue(paramName)\n\tif val == \"\" {\n\t\treturn defaultValue, nil\n\t}\n\tresult, err := parseTime(val)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn time.Time{}, fmt.Errorf(\"invalid time value for '%s': %w\", paramName, err)\n\t}\n\treturn result, nil\n}\n\nfunc parseTime(s string) (time.Time, error) {\n\tif t, err := strconv.ParseFloat(s, 64); err == nil {\n\t\ts, ns := math.Modf(t)\n\t\tns = math.Round(ns*1000) / 1000\n\t\treturn time.Unix(int64(s), int64(ns*float64(time.Second))).UTC(), nil\n\t}\n\tif t, err := time.Parse(time.RFC3339Nano, s); err == nil {\n\t\treturn t, nil\n\t}\n\n\t// Stdlib's time parser can only handle 4 digit years. As a workaround until\n\t// that is fixed we want to at least support our own boundary times.\n\t// Context: https://github.com/prometheus/client_golang/issues/614\n\t// Upstream issue: https://github.com/golang/go/issues/20555\n\tswitch s {\n\tcase minTimeFormatted:\n\t\treturn MinTime, nil\n\tcase maxTimeFormatted:\n\t\treturn MaxTime, nil\n\t}\n\treturn time.Time{}, fmt.Errorf(\"cannot parse %q to a valid timestamp\", s)\n}\n\nfunc parseDuration(s string) (time.Duration, error) {\n\tif d, err := strconv.ParseFloat(s, 64); err == nil {\n\t\tts := d * float64(time.Second)\n\t\tif ts > float64(math.MaxInt64) || ts < float64(math.MinInt64) {\n\t\t\treturn 0, fmt.Errorf(\"cannot parse %q to a valid duration. It overflows int64\", s)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn time.Duration(ts), nil\n\t}\n\tif d, err := model.ParseDuration(s); err == nil {\n\t\treturn time.Duration(d), nil\n\t}\n\treturn 0, fmt.Errorf(\"cannot parse %q to a valid duration\", s)\n}\n\nfunc parseMatchersParam(matchers []string) ([][]*labels.Matcher, error) {\n\tmatcherSets, err := parser.ParseMetricSelectors(matchers)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\nOUTER:\n\tfor _, ms := range matcherSets {\n\t\tfor _, lm := range ms {\n\t\t\tif lm != nil && !lm.Matches(\"\") {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue OUTER\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn nil, errors.New(\"match[] must contain at least one non-empty matcher\")\n\t}\n\treturn matcherSets, nil\n}\n\n// parseLimitParam returning 0 means no limit is to be applied.\nfunc parseLimitParam(limitStr string) (limit int, err error) {\n\tif limitStr == \"\" {\n\t\treturn limit, nil\n\t}\n\n\tlimit, err = strconv.Atoi(limitStr)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn limit, err\n\t}\n\tif limit < 0 {\n\t\treturn limit, errors.New(\"limit must be non-negative\")\n\t}\n\n\treturn limit, nil\n}\n\n// toHintLimit increases the API limit, as returned by parseLimitParam, by 1.\n// This allows for emitting warnings when the results are truncated.\nfunc toHintLimit(limit int) int {\n\t// 0 means no limit and avoid int overflow\n\tif limit > 0 && limit < math.MaxInt {\n\t\treturn limit + 1\n\t}\n\treturn limit\n}\n\n// truncateResults truncates result for queryRange() and query().\n// No truncation for other types(Scalars or Strings).\nfunc truncateResults(result *promql.Result, limit int) (*promql.Result, bool) {\n\tisTruncated := false\n\n\tswitch v := result.Value.(type) {\n\tcase promql.Matrix:\n\t\tif len(v) > limit {\n\t\t\tresult.Value = v[:limit]\n\t\t\tisTruncated = true\n\t\t}\n\tcase promql.Vector:\n\t\tif len(v) > limit {\n\t\t\tresult.Value = v[:limit]\n\t\t\tisTruncated = true\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Return the modified result. Unchanged for other types.\n\treturn result, isTruncated\n}\n\n// Silence represents a silence in the Alertmanager.\ntype Silence struct {\n\tID        string // Silence represents a silence in the Alertmanager.
type Silence struct {
	ID        string            `json:"id,omitempty"`
	Matchers  []SilenceMatcher  `json:"matchers"`
	StartsAt  time.Time         `json:"startsAt"`
	EndsAt    time.Time         `json:"endsAt"`
	CreatedBy string            `json:"createdBy"`
	Comment   string            `json:"comment"`
}

// SilenceMatcher matches labels for silencing alerts.
type SilenceMatcher struct {
	Name    string `json:"name"`
	Value   string `json:"value"`
	IsRegex bool   `json:"isRegex"`
}

// BulkSilenceRequest represents a request to create multiple silences.
type BulkSilenceRequest struct {
	Silences []Silence `json:"silences"`
}

// BulkSilenceResponse represents the response from creating multiple silences.
type BulkSilenceResponse struct {
	SilenceIDs []string `json:"silenceIds"`
}

// BulkSilenceError represents an error response with detailed failure information.
type BulkSilenceError struct {
	Index   int    `json:"index"`
	Message string `json:"message"`
}

// validateSilence validates a silence object.
func validateSilence(s *Silence) error {
	if s == nil {
		return errors.New("silence cannot be nil")
	}
	if len(s.Matchers) == 0 {
		return errors.New("silence must have at least one matcher")
	}
	for i, m := range s.Matchers {
		if m.Name == "" {
			return fmt.Errorf("matcher %d: name cannot be empty", i)
		}
	}
	if s.StartsAt.IsZero() {
		return errors.New("startsAt cannot be empty")
	}
	if s.EndsAt.IsZero() {
		return errors.New("endsAt cannot be empty")
	}
	if s.EndsAt.Before(s.StartsAt) {
		return errors.New("endsAt must be after startsAt")
	}
	return nil
}

import re
import sys

# Simple syntax check - verify Go code structure
def check_go_file(filepath):
    with open(filepath, 'r') as f:
        content = f.read()
    
    # Check for common issues
    issues = []
    
    # Check function declarations
    funcs = re.findall(r'func \(([^)]+)\) (\w+)\(([^)]*)\) (\w+Result)', content)
    if not funcs:
        issues.append('No functions with proper signatures found')
    
    # Check type definitions
    types = re.findall(r'type (\w+) struct', content)
    print(f'Found {len(types)} struct types: {types}')
    
    # Check for balance in braces
    open_braces = content.count('{')
    close_braces = content.count('}')
    if open_braces != close_braces:
        issues.append(f'Unbalanced braces: {open_braces} open, {close_braces} close')
    
    return issues

issues_api = check_go_file('web/api/v1/api.go')
issues_test = check_go_file('web/api/v1/silences_bulk_test.go')

if issues_api:
    print(f'API file issues: {issues_api}')
else:
    print('API file syntax OK')

if issues_test:
    print(f'Test file issues: {issues_test}')
else:
    print('Test file syntax OK')
"
